# <a name="whats-new-in-excel-javascript-api-12"></a><span data-ttu-id="446ea-103">Quais são as novidades na API JavaScript do Excel 1.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="446ea-103">What's new in Excel JavaScript API 1.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="446ea-104">ExcelApi 1,2 adicionado suporte para filtragem de tabela e acesso a funções internas do Excel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="446ea-104">ExcelApi 1.2 added support for table filtering and access to built-in Excel functions.</span></span>
